### #004 [RAW] SUPERVISOR_KICKOFF_RAW_OUTPUT

<details>
<summary>Open raw LLM output</summary>

```text
{
  "supervisor_decision": {
    "action": "start_run",
    "global_objective": {
      "objective_layers": ["missed_priority", "energy_total"],
      "explanation": {
        "primary": "Minimize missed priority to ensure valuable task coverage.",
        "secondary": "Minimize total energy usage to reduce resource consumption."
      }
    },
    "next_contract": {
      "contract_type": "initial_construction",
      "objective_layers": ["missed_priority", "energy_total"],
      "feasibility_control": {
        "mode": "strict",
        "relaxation_ratios": []
      },
      "situation_assessment": {
        "summary": "Instance T100 has 100 tasks, 6 agents, with high spatial clustering (0.83) and no constraint tensions (time window, energy tightness none). All tasks are skill-coverable, and most have multiple capable agents. Priority mass is 198 with 36 high-priority tasks. The problem is well-suited for constructing a feasible solution covering all tasks and then optimizing energy.",
        "reasoning_from_evidence": "Observation O0 shows cluster_strength=0.83, indicating tasks are spatially clustered, enabling efficient routing. No negative slack or tight energy constraints. Capable count distribution shows that 41 tasks can be done by 5 agents, 8 by all 6, so flexibility is high. With sufficient resources (10 step calls, 20 solver calls, 300s, 2000 iters), we expect to find a feasible solution covering all high-priority tasks and then reduce energy."
      },
      "target_intents": [
        {
          "intent_id": "cover_high_priority",
          "intent_type": "construction",
          "evidence_refs": ["O0"],
          "expected_effects": [
            {"metric": "missed_priority", "direction": "decrease"},
            {"metric": "unassigned_count", "direction": "decrease"},
            {"metric": "energy_total", "direction": "maintain"}
          ],
          "rationale": "Initial construction should prioritize covering all high-priority tasks using capable agents while respecting constraints. This establishes a feasible baseline that can be refined later."
        }
      ],
      "protected_metrics": [],
      "resource_policy": {
        "min_actions": 1,
        "max_actions": 10,
        "max_iters": 2000,
        "max_time_sec": 300.0
      },
      "exit_conditions": {
        "success": [
          {
            "condition_id": "feasible_found",
            "source": "best_feasible.exists",
            "op": "==",
            "value": true,
            "window": 1
          }
        ],
        "failure": [
          {
            "condition_id": "actions_exhausted",
            "source": "progress.solver_actions",
            "op": ">=",
            "value": 10,
            "window": 1
          },
          {
            "condition_id": "time_exhausted",
            "source": "progress.time_used_sec",
            "op": ">=",
            "value": 300.0,
            "window": 1
          }
        ]
      },
      "explanation": {
        "strategy": "Use strict feasibility to build a solution covering all tasks, then refine to minimize energy. With abundant resources and no constraint tightness, strict mode is safe."
      }
    }
  }
}
```
